<s> at the corners of london squares they gave out as the sun went down a perfume sweeter than the honey bees had taken a perfume that stirred a yearning unnamable in the hearts of forsytes and their peers taking the cool after dinner in the precincts of those gardens to which they alone had keys <\s>
<s> and that yearning made them linger amidst the dim shapes of flower beds in the failing daylight made them turn and turn and turn again as though lovers were waiting for them waiting for the last light to die away under the shadow of the branches <\s>

<s> black thoughts about soames mingled with the faintest hopes <\s>
<s> on the friday night he got drunk so greatly was he affected <\s>
<s> but on saturday morning the true stock exchange instinct triumphed within him <\s>
<s> owing some hundreds which by no possibility could he pay he went into town and put them all on concertina for the saltown borough handicap <\s>

<s> if it didn't come up well then damme the old man would have to pay <\s>

<s> twice only did husband and wife exchange remarks on the way <\s>

<s> they were standing in one of the long french windows overlooking the river <\s>
<s> windows that summer were open all day long and all night too and day and night the scents of flowers and trees came in the hot scent of parching grass and the cool scent of the heavy dews <\s>
<s> to the eye of the observant dartie his two guests did not appear to be making much running standing there close together without a word <\s>
<s> bosinney was a hungry looking creature not much go about him <\s>
<s> he left them to winifred however and busied himself to order the dinner <\s>
<s> a forsyte will require good if not delicate feeding but a dartie will tax the resources of a crown and sceptre <\s>
<s> living as he does from hand to mouth nothing is too good for him to eat and he will eat it <\s>

<s> to stint yourself is the mark of a fool not of a dartie <\s>

<s> the feature of the feast was unquestionably the red mullet <\s>

<s> nothing else calls for remark except the payment of the bill by dartie <\s>
<s> he had made himself extremely agreeable throughout the meal his bold admiring stare seldom abandoning irene's face and figure <\s>

<s> he expected to have caught her out in some little game with bosinney but not a bit of it she kept up her end remarkably well <\s>
<s> as for that architect chap he was as glum as a bear with a sore head winifred could barely get a word out of him he ate nothing but he certainly took his liquor and his face kept getting whiter and his eyes looked queer <\s>
<s> it was all very amusing <\s>
<s> for dartie himself was in capital form and talked freely with a certain poignancy being no fool <\s>

<s> a forsyte will require good if not delicate feeding but a dartie will tax the resources of a crown and sceptre <\s>

<s> he expected to have caught her out in some little game with bosinney but not a bit of it she kept up her end remarkably well <\s>

<s> it was all very amusing <\s>
